 aise hi shabd hai - repo rate, reverse repo rate or siararrepo raterosemara ke kaamkaaj ke liye bainkon ko rupayon kii jarurat padati he
 In such a situation, it is the easiest option for him to take a loan from the country's central bank i
e
 the Reserve Bank of India (RBI)
 is tarah ke rin par rigerv bank jis dar se unase byaaj vasuul karata he, use repo rate kehete hai
 In other words, the rate at which the Reserve Bank lends money to other commercial banks and financial institutions is called repo rate
 jab bainkon ko kam dar par rin uplabdh hoga, ve bhi graahakon ko aakarshith karne ke liye apni byaaj daron ko kam kar sakate hai, taaki rin lene vaale graahakon main adhik se adhik badhotaree kii ja sake, or adhik rakam rin par di ja sake
 Similarly, if the Reserve Bank increases the repo rate, it will become expensive for banks to take loans, and they will also raise the interest rates charged from their customers
 reverse repo rateyah repo rate se vipareet he
 Sometimes when banks are left with a large amount of money after work, they keep that amount on the Reserve Bank, on which the RBI pays them interest
 ab rigerv bank is rakam par jis dar se byaaj adaa karata he, use reverse repo rate kehete hai
 That is, reverse repo is the rate at which other banks lend money to the Reserve Bank
 darasal, reverse repo rate market main cash flo ko niyantrit karne main kaam aati he
 Whenever there is too much cash in the market, RBI increases the reverse repo rate, so that banks deposit their money with it to earn more interest, and thus less money will be left in the possession of the banks in the market

 Pongal is the symbol of the sun being Uttarayan from Dakshinayan
 is baar pongal kaa tyohaar 15 janvari se 18 farvari tak manaaya jayega
 The people of Tamil Nadu celebrate the harvest festival Pongal with gaiety and show their gratitude to the rain, sun and cattle
 log subah jaldi uthakar nae kapade pahante hai or mandiron main jaakar bhagwaan kii aradhana karte hai
 The aroma of cashew, almond and cardamom fried in ghee makes the whole house smell as traditional dish is prepared from rice, jaggery and gram dal
 chakrai pongal kii saamagree doodh main ubaal kar log 'pongalo pongal', 'pongalo pongal' bolte hai
 Pongal in Tamil language means boiling well
 yani ki chaaval, gud or daal se bane is bhoga ko acchhee tarah ubalkar bhagwaan surya ko arpit kiya jaataa he
 To show gratitude to Lord Surya, he is offered a dish of Pongal, after which he is accepted as a Prasad
 log ek duusare ko pongal kii badhai dete hai or chakrai pongal kaa aadan-pradaan karte hai
 The festival of Pongal is celebrated for four days
 pehla din bhogi hota he, is din log puraane kapade, dari aadi chizon ke jalaate hai or gharon kaa rang-rogan karte hai
 The second day is the main festival of Pongal, celebrated on the first day of the Tamil month of Thai
 teesraa din mattu pongal hota he, jab gaay, belon ko nahalaakar unke singon ko ranga jaataa he or unki puja kii jaati he
 The women feed the birds with dyed rice and pray for the welfare of their brothers
 rajya ke kuch hisson main sand ko pakadaney ke khel - jalikattu kaa bhi aayojan kiya jaataa he
 Kannam Pongal is celebrated on the fourth day
 is din log apane mitron or rishtedaaron ke ghar jaakar unase mulaakaat karte hai or ghoomane-phirane jate hai

 In fact, Facial Superimposition and Digital Facial Imposition is such a modern technology through which any human skull in the lab can be given its appearance
 bas shart ye he jisaki maut kaa shaq he uski ek tasviir milan ke liye forensik exparts ke paas maujuud ho
 Nasal index i
e
 nasal texture, facial index i
e
 facial texture, eye index ie eye texture, glabella index ie frontal texture and zyzion ie facial width are studied in depth
 kisi bhi shaks ke chehre ko dobaaraa banane ke liye forensik sains main dwi aayam yaa phir tri aayam takanic kaa istemaal kiya jaataa he
 In double dimension or two dimensional technique, the person's face is reconstructed with the help of a photograph of the person before he died or a radiograph of the head skull
 tri-aayam yaa thri diemension takanic main mare hue shaks ke kapaal yani sir kii haddi ke tukdon kii madad se uskaa cheharaa banaaya jaataa he yaa phir mitti se bhi uske chehre kaa model taiyaar kiya jaataa he yaa phir computer par uske chehre kii image banaai jaati he
 Superimposition technique is not always used in forensic science, because in this technique, the person who makes a face must have some knowledge of the structure of the bones of the deceased
